***вдова.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вдова.html>вдова</a> (4861)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vьdova</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁widʰéwh₂</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">widow</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Witwe</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">veuve</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">viuda</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">vedova</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hindi" class="extiw" title="w:Hindi">Hindi</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="hi">विद्वा</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vidvā</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вдова.html>вдова́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vdová</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вдова.html>вдовы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вдова.html>вдо́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вдова.html>вдо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>widow</li></ol>

***вдогонку.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вдогонку.html>вдого́нку</a> (9967)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гонка.html>го́нку</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gónku</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + the root of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:догонять.html>догоня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dogonjátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to overtake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вдогонку.html>вдого́нку</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vdogónku</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> after <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in pursuit of</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуститься.html>пусти́ться</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вдогонку.html>вдого́нку</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pustítʹsja <b>vdogónku</b> (za)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rush/dash (after; in pursuit of)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:послать.html>посла́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:письмо.html>письмо́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вдогонку.html>вдого́нку</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">poslátʹ pisʹmó <b>vdogónku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to send on a letter</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крикнуть.html>кри́кнуть</a> кому́-либо <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вдогонку.html>вдого́нку</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kríknutʹ komú-libo <b>vdogónku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to call after someone</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***вдохновлённый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вдохновлённый.html>вдохновлённый</a> (20537)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вдохновлённый.html>вдохновлённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vdoxnovljónnyj</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вдохнуть.html>вдохну́ть</a> (8882)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дохнуть.html>дохну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">doxnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вдохнуть.html>вдохну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vdoxnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вдыхать.html>вдыха́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to inhale, to breathe in
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вдохнуть.html>вдохну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свежий.html>све́жий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воздух.html>во́здух</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vdoxnútʹ</b> svéžij vózdux</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to inhale (breathe in) fresh air</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вдребезги.html>вдре́безги</a> (10902)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вдребезги.html>вдре́безги</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vdrébezgi</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pieces, into smithereens</li></ol>
<hr><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мелкий.html>ме́лкие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>части</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:осколок.html>оско́лки</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вдумываться.html>вду́мывающийся</a> (28795)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вдумываться.html>вду́мывающийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vdúmyvajuščijsja</span>)

***вдыхать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вдыхать.html>вдыха́ть</a> (8889)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ды́хать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dýxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вдыхать.html>вдыха́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vdyxátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вдохнуть.html>вдохну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to inhale, to breathe in
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вдыхать.html>вдыха́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свежий.html>све́жий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воздух.html>во́здух</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vdyxátʹ</b> svéžij vózdux</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to inhale (breathe in) fresh air</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***вегетативный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вегетативный.html>вегетати́вный</a> (20356)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">vegetativ</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вегетативный.html>вегетати́вный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vegetatívnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>vegetative, autonomic</li></ol>

***ведать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ведать.html>ведать</a> (3987)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*věděti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wóyde</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to know</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, perfect of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*weyd-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to see, to know</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведать.html>ве́дать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">védatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic or poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to know <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">be certain or sure about something</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to govern, to manage, to control
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>Кто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нас</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ведать.html>ве́дает</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пожарный.html>пожа́рной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:безопасность.html>безопа́сностью</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kto u nas <b>védajet</b> požárnoj bezopásnostʹju?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Who manages the fire safety among us? (<i>instrumental case)</i></span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голова́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ведать.html>ве́дает</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:волость.html>во́лость</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Golová <b>védajet</b> vólostʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">A leader governs a volost. (<i>archaic transitive usage</i>)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to know</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>знать</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">znatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">common term</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to govern, manage</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заведовать.html>заве́довать</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zavédovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:управлять.html>управля́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">upravljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***ведение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ведение.html>ведение</a> (7287)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведать.html>ве́дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">védatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to know, to be in charge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ение</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-enije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*weyd-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведение.html>ве́дение</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">védenije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведение.html>ве́дения</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведение.html>ве́дения</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведение.html>ве́дений</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>knowledge, lore</li>
<li>authority, charge, competence</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">переводове́дение</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perevodovédenije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:краеведческий.html>краеве́дческий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">krajevédčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вед-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ved-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to conduct, direct</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*weǵʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to move</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведение.html>веде́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vedénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведение.html>веде́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведение.html>веде́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведение.html>веде́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>directing, leadership
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ведение.html>ведение</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:бухгалтерский.html>бухга́лтерских</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́г</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vedenije</b> (bugálterskix/buhálterskix) knig</i> ― <span class="e-translation">bookkeeping</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ведение.html>ведение</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйство.html>хозя́йства</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vedenije</b> xozjájstva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">housekeeping</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ведение.html>ведение</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>огня́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vedenije</b> ognjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">firing (weapons)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>management, managing</li>
